### Round 3: Monaco Grand Prix
*Date: 1989-05-07*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 8: British Grand Prix
*Date: 1989-07-16*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting Elo | Change | New Elo | vs Teammate |
